### <a name="aspnet-chart-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-599">ASP.NET 图表控件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-599">ASP.NET Chart Control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-600">ASP.NET*图表*控件扩展.NET Framework 中的数据可视化产品/服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-600">The ASP.NET *Chart* control expands the data-visualization offerings in the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-601">使用*图表*控件，可以创建具有复杂的统计或财务分析使用直观和极具视觉表现力的图表的 ASP.NET 页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-601">Using the *Chart* control, you can create ASP.NET pages that have intuitive and visually compelling charts for complex statistical or financial analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-602">ASP.NET*图表*控件作为外接程序引入到.NET Framework 版本 3.5 SP1 版本，.NET Framework 4 版本的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-602">The ASP.NET *Chart* control was introduced as an add-on to the .NET Framework version 3.5 SP1 release and is part of the .NET Framework 4 release.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-603">控件包括以下功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-603">The control includes the following features:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-604">35 种不同的图表类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-604">35 distinct chart types.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-605">无限的数量的图表区、 标题、 图例和批注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-605">An unlimited number of chart areas, titles, legends, and annotations.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-606">各种不同的所有图表元素的外观设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-606">A wide variety of appearance settings for all chart elements.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-607">对于大多数图表类型的三维支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-607">3-D support for most chart types.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-608">可以自动适应数据点周围的智能数据标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-608">Smart data labels that can automatically fit around data points.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-609">条带线、 刻度分隔线和对数缩放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-609">Strip lines, scale breaks, and logarithmic scaling.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-610">包含 50 多个用于数据分析和转换的财务和统计公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-610">More than 50 financial and statistical formulas for data analysis and transformation.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-611">简单绑定和操作的图表数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-611">Simple binding and manipulation of chart data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-612">对支持常见的数据格式，如日期、 时间和货币。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-612">Support for common data formats such as dates, times, and currency.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-613">以实现交互性和事件驱动的自定义，包括客户端的支持，请单击使用 Ajax 的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-613">Support for interactivity and event-driven customization, including client click events using Ajax.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-614">状态管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-614">State management.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-615">二进制流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-615">Binary streaming.</span></span>

### <a name="filtering-data-with-the-queryextender-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-635">用 QueryExtender 控件筛选数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-635">Filtering Data with the QueryExtender Control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-636">创建数据驱动的网页开发人员非常常见的任务是筛选数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-636">A very common task for developers who create data-driven Web pages is to filter data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-637">这通常已由执行构建*其中*子句中的数据源控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-637">This traditionally has been performed by building *Where* clauses in data source controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-638">此方法可能很复杂，在某些情况下*其中*语法不允许您充分利用基础数据库的完整功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-638">This approach can be complicated, and in some cases the *Where* syntax does not let you take advantage of the full functionality of the underlying database.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-639">若要简化筛选操作，一个新*QueryExtender*已在 ASP.NET 4 中添加控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-639">To make filtering easier, a new *QueryExtender* control has been added in ASP.NET 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-640">此控件可以添加到*EntityDataSource*或*LinqDataSource*以便筛选这些控件返回的数据的控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-640">This control can be added to *EntityDataSource* or *LinqDataSource* controls in order to filter the data returned by these controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-641">因为*QueryExtender*控件依赖于 LINQ，则将数据发送到页上，这会导致非常高效地执行操作之前筛选器在数据库服务器上应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-641">Because the *QueryExtender* control relies on LINQ, the filter is applied on the database server before the data is sent to the page, which results in very efficient operations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-642">*QueryExtender*控件支持的各种筛选器选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-642">The *QueryExtender* control supports a variety of filter options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-643">以下部分介绍了这些选项，并提供有关如何使用它们的示例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-643">The following sections describe these options and provide examples of how to use them.</span></span>

#### <a name="search"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-644">搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-644">Search</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-645">搜索选项时， *QueryExtender*控件中指定的字段执行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-645">For the search option, the *QueryExtender* control performs a search in specified fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-646">在以下示例中，该控件使用 TextBoxSearch 控件和对其内容中的搜索中输入的文本`ProductName`并`Supplier.CompanyName`中返回的数据的列*LinqDataSource*控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-646">In the following example, the control uses the text that is entered in the TextBoxSearch control and searches for its contents in the `ProductName` and `Supplier.CompanyName` columns in the data that is returned from the *LinqDataSource* control.</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample61.aspx)]

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-647">范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-647">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-648">范围选项类似于搜索选项，但指定的值来定义范围的对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-648">The range option is similar to the search option, but specifies a pair of values to define the range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-649">在以下示例中， *QueryExtender*控制搜索`UnitPrice`中返回的数据列*LinqDataSource*控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-649">In the following example, the *QueryExtender* control searches the `UnitPrice` column in the data returned from the *LinqDataSource* control.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-650">从页面上的 TextBoxFrom 和 TextBoxTo 控件中读取范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-650">The range is read from the TextBoxFrom and TextBoxTo controls on the page.</span></span>

### <a name="html-encoded-code-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-663">Html 编码的代码表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-663">Html Encoded Code Expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-664">使用依赖于 （特别是使用 ASP.NET MVC) 的某些 ASP.NET 站点`<%` =  `expression %>` （通常称为"代码片段"） 的语法将一些文本写入响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-664">Some ASP.NET sites (especially with ASP.NET MVC) rely heavily on using `<%`= `expression %>` syntax (often called "code nuggets") to write some text to the response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-665">当您使用的代码表达式时，它很容易忘记进行 HTML 编码的文本，如果文本来自用户输入，它可能会导致页打开到 XSS （跨站点脚本） 攻击。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-665">When you use code expressions, it is easy to forget to HTML-encode the text, If the text comes from user input, it can leave pages open to an XSS (Cross Site Scripting) attack.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-666">ASP.NET 4 引入了以下新代码表达式的语法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-666">ASP.NET 4 introduces the following new syntax for code expressions:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample66.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-667">此语法使用写入到响应时，HTML 编码，默认情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-667">This syntax uses HTML encoding by default when writing to the response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-668">此新表达式有效地转换为以下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-668">This new expression effectively translates to the following:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample67.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-669">例如， &lt;%:请求"/userinput&gt"%&gt;执行 HTML 编码的值*请求"/userinput&gt"* 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-669">For example, &lt;%: Request["UserInput"] %&gt; performs HTML encoding on the value of *Request["UserInput"]*.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-670">此功能旨在使其可以替换为旧语法的所有实例的新语法，以便将无需再决定每个步骤要使用哪一个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-670">The goal of this feature is to make it possible to replace all instances of the old syntax with the new syntax so that you are not forced to decide at every step which one to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-671">但是，一些情况下要输出的文本要作为 HTML 或已经进行了编码，在这种情况下这可能会导致双重解码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-671">However, there are cases in which the text being output is meant to be HTML or is already encoded, in which case this could lead to double encoding.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-672">对于这些情况下，ASP.NET 4 引入了一个新的接口*IHtmlString*，具体实现，以及*HtmlString*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-672">For those cases, ASP.NET 4 introduces a new interface, *IHtmlString*, along with a concrete implementation, *HtmlString*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-673">这些类型的实例，您可以指示，返回值是已正确编码 （或否则检查） 用于显示为 HTML，并，因此值不应为 HTML 编码试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-673">Instances of these types let you indicate that the return value is already properly encoded (or otherwise examined) for displaying as HTML, and that therefore the value should not be HTML-encoded again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-674">例如，以下不应为 （并不是） 编码的 HTML:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-674">For example, the following should not be (and is not) HTML encoded:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample68.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-675">ASP.NET 4 运行时，已更新为使用此新语法，以便它们不是双编码的但仅限于 ASP.NET MVC 2 帮助器方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-675">ASP.NET MVC 2 helper methods have been updated to work with this new syntax so that they are not double encoded, but only when you are running ASP.NET 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-676">运行使用 ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 的应用程序时，则此新语法无效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-676">This new syntax does not work when you run an application using ASP.NET 3.5 SP1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-680">同样，此语法不执行 JavaScript 编码，例如当您创建基于用户输入的 JavaScript 字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-680">Likewise, this syntax does not perform JavaScript encoding, such as when you create a JavaScript string based on user input.</span></span>

### <a name="project-template-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-681">项目模板更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-681">Project Template Changes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-682">在 ASP.NET 的早期版本中，使用 Visual Studio 来创建新网站项目或 Web 应用程序项目时生成的项目包含仅 Default.aspx 页上，默认值`Web.config`文件，和`App_Data`文件夹中，按如下所示图：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-682">In earlier versions of ASP.NET, when you use Visual Studio to create a new Web Site project or Web Application project, the resulting projects contain only a Default.aspx page, a default `Web.config` file, and the `App_Data` folder, as shown in the following illustration:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1A"></a>![](overview/_static/image4.png)

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-683">Visual Studio 还支持空网站项目类型，不包含任何文件根本下, 图中所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-683">Visual Studio also supports an Empty Web Site project type, which contains no files at all, as shown in the following figure:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1B"></a>![](overview/_static/image5.png)

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-684">结果是，对于初学者，很少指导如何构建生产型 Web 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-684">The result is that for the beginner, there is very little guidance on how to build a production Web application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-685">因此，ASP.NET 4 引入了三个新模板，另一个为空的 Web 应用程序项目，每个 Web 应用程序和网站项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-685">Therefore, ASP.NET 4 introduces three new templates, one for an empty Web application project, and one each for a Web Application and Web Site project.</span></span>

#### <a name="empty-web-application-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-686">空 Web 应用程序模板</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-686">Empty Web Application Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-687">顾名思义，空 Web 应用程序模板是一个精简的 Web 应用程序项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-687">As the name suggests, the Empty Web Application template is a stripped-down Web Application project.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-688">下图中所示，可以从 Visual Studio 新项目对话框中，选择此项目模板：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-688">You select this project template from the Visual Studio New Project dialog box, as shown in the following figure:</span></span>

[![](overview/_static/image7.png)](overview/_static/image6.png)

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-689">([单击此项可查看原尺寸图像](overview/_static/image8.png))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-689">([Click to view full-size image](overview/_static/image8.png))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-690">创建空的 ASP.NET Web 应用程序时，Visual Studio 将创建以下文件夹布局：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-690">When you create an Empty ASP.NET Web Application, Visual Studio creates the following folder layout:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-712">项目模板的这些更改的目的是提供有关如何开始构建新的 Web 应用程序的指导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-712">The intention of these changes to the project templates is to provide guidance on how to start building a new Web application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-713">使用语义正确，严格 XHTML 1.0 符合标记和使用 CSS 指定的布局，在模板中的页表示用于构建 ASP.NET 4 Web 应用程序的最佳实践。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-713">With semantically correct, strict XHTML 1.0-compliant markup and with layout that is specified using CSS, the pages in the templates represent best practices for building ASP.NET 4 Web applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-714">默认页还具有您可以轻松地自定义的两列布局。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-714">The default pages also have a two-column layout that you can easily customize.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-715">例如，假设为新的 Web 应用程序想要更改的某些颜色并插入我的 ASP.NET 应用程序徽标代替你公司的徽标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-715">For example, imagine that for a new Web Application you want to change some of the colors and insert your company logo in place of the My ASP.NET Application logo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-716">若要执行此操作，创建一个新目录下的`Content`来存储你的徽标图像：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-716">To do this, you create a new directory under `Content` to store your logo image:</span></span>

### <a name="css-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-722">CSS 改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-722">CSS Improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-723">在 ASP.NET 4 中主要领域之一是工作的帮助呈现 HTML 与最新的 HTML 标准兼容的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-723">One of the major areas of work in ASP.NET 4 has been to help render HTML that is compliant with the latest HTML standards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-724">这包括对 ASP.NET Web 服务器控件如何使用 CSS 样式的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-724">This includes changes to how ASP.NET Web server controls use CSS styles.</span></span>

#### <a name="compatibility-setting-for-rendering"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-725">呈现的兼容性设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-725">Compatibility Setting for Rendering</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-726">默认情况下，当 Web 应用程序或网站以.NET Framework 4 为目标*controlRenderingCompatibilityVersion*的属性*页面*元素设置为"4.0"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-726">By default, when a Web application or Web site targets the .NET Framework 4, the *controlRenderingCompatibilityVersion* attribute of the *pages* element is set to "4.0".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-727">此元素定义在计算机级别`Web.config`文件，默认情况下适用于所有 ASP.NET 4 应用程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-727">This element is defined in the machine-level `Web.config` file and by default applies to all ASP.NET 4 applications:</span></span>

[!code-xml[Main](overview/samples/sample69.xml)]

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-728">值*controlRenderingCompatibility*是一个字符串，它允许潜在的新版本定义在将来的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-728">The value for *controlRenderingCompatibility* is a string, which allows potential new version definitions in future releases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-729">在当前版本中，此属性支持以下值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-729">In the current release, the following values are supported for this property:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-730">"3.5".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-730">"3.5".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-731">此设置指示旧式呈现和标记。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-731">This setting indicates legacy rendering and markup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-732">呈现的控件的标记是 100%向后兼容，以及设置的*xhtmlConformance*遵循属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-732">Markup rendered by controls is 100% backward compatible, and the setting of the *xhtmlConformance* property is honored.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-733">"4.0".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-733">"4.0".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-734">如果该属性具有此设置，ASP.NET Web 服务器控件执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-734">If the property has this setting, ASP.NET Web server controls do the following:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-735">*XhtmlConformance*属性始终被视为"Strict"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-735">The *xhtmlConformance* property is always treated as "Strict".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-736">因此，控件将呈现 XHTML 1.0 Strict 标记。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-736">As a result, controls render XHTML 1.0 Strict markup.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-737">禁用非输入控件不再呈现无效样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-737">Disabling non-input controls no longer renders invalid styles.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-738">*div*现在样式围绕隐藏的字段的元素，以便它们不会干扰用户创建 CSS 规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-738">*div* elements around hidden fields are now styled so they do not interfere with user-created CSS rules.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-739">菜单控件呈现在语义上正确并且符合辅助功能准则的标记。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-739">Menu controls render markup that is semantically correct and compliant with accessibility guidelines.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-740">验证控件不呈现内联样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-740">Validation controls do not render inline styles.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-741">控制以前呈现边框 ="0"(派生自 ASP.NET 控件*表*控制和 ASP.NET*映像*控件) 不再呈现此属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-741">Controls that previously rendered border="0" (controls that derive from the ASP.NET *Table* control, and the ASP.NET *Image* control) no longer render this attribute.</span></span>

### <a name="hiding-div-elements-around-hidden-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-755">隐藏 div 元素周围隐藏字段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-755">Hiding div Elements Around Hidden Fields</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-798">请注意是否您设置*RepeatLayout*到*OrderedList*或*UnorderedList*，则*RepeatDirection*属性不再可用，并且将如果标记或代码中设置该属性，则引发运行时异常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-798">Note If you set *RepeatLayout* to *OrderedList* or *UnorderedList*, the *RepeatDirection* property can no longer be used and will throw an exception at run time if the property has been set within your markup or code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-799">属性将具有任何值，因为这些控件的可视布局而使用 CSS 进行定义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-799">The property would have no value because the visual layout of these controls is defined using CSS instead.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429272"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304646"></a>

### <a name="menu-control-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-800">菜单控件改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-800">Menu Control Improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-801">在 ASP.NET 4 中前,*菜单*呈现控件的一系列 HTML 表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-801">Before ASP.NET 4, the *Menu* control rendered a series of HTML tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-802">这变得更困难，应用 CSS 样式设置内联属性之外，也是不符合可访问性标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-802">This made it more difficult to apply CSS styles outside of setting inline properties and was also not compliant with accessibility standards.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-803">在 ASP.NET 4 中，该控件现在呈现 HTML 中使用的未排序的列表和列表元素组成的语义标记。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-803">In ASP.NET 4, the control now renders HTML using semantic markup that consists of an unordered list and list elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-804">下面的示例演示在 ASP.NET 页面的标记*菜单*控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-804">The following example shows markup in an ASP.NET page for the *Menu* control.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-806">除了呈现的改进，已使用焦点管理得到改进的菜单的键盘导航。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-806">In addition to rendering improvements, keyboard navigation of the menu has been improved using focus management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-807">当*菜单*控件获得焦点，则可以使用箭头键导航元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-807">When the *Menu* control gets focus, you can use the arrow keys to navigate elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-808">*菜单*控件现在还将附加可访问富 internet 应用程序 (ARIA) 角色和属性 follo[wing](http://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices/#menu "菜单 ARIA 准则")为了改进可访问性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-808">The *Menu* control also now attaches accessible rich internet applications (ARIA) roles and attributes follo[wing the](http://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices/#menu "Menu ARIA guidelines")for improved accessibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-809">样式块中位于顶部的页上，而不是根据呈现的 HTML 元素呈现菜单控件的样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-809">Styles for the menu control are rendered in a style block at the top of the page, rather than in line with the rendered HTML elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-810">如果你想要完全控制控件的样式，则可以设置新*IncludeStyleBlock*属性设置为*false*，在这种情况下，将不发出样式块。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-810">If you want to take full control over the styling for the control, you can set the new *IncludeStyleBlock* property to *false*, in which case the style block is not emitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-811">若要使用此属性的一种方法是使用 Visual Studio 设计器中的自动套用格式功能设置菜单的外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-811">One way to use this property is to use the auto-format feature in the Visual Studio designer to set the appearance of the menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-812">然后可以运行页、 开放源代码的页，然后将呈现的样式块复制到外部 CSS 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-812">You can then run the page, open the page source, and then copy the rendered style block to an external CSS file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-813">在 Visual Studio 中，撤消样式设置和组*IncludeStyleBlock*到*false*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-813">In Visual Studio, undo the styling and set *IncludeStyleBlock* to *false*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-814">结果是在外部样式表中使用样式定义菜单外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-814">The result is that the menu appearance is defined using styles in an external style sheet.</span></span>

## <a name="aspnet-mvc"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-830">ASP.NET MVC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-830">ASP.NET MVC</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-831">ASP.NET MVC 是作为外接程序框架到 ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 中引入 2009 年 3 月。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-831">ASP.NET MVC was introduced as an add-on framework to ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 in March 2009.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-832">Visual Studio 2010 包括 ASP.NET MVC 2，其中包括新特性和功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-832">Visual Studio 2010 includes ASP.NET MVC 2, which includes new features and capabilities.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429275"></a>

### <a name="areas-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-833">区域支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-833">Areas Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-834">区域可以组控制器和视图为部分以相对其他部分隔离的大型应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-834">Areas let you group controllers and views into sections of a large application in relative isolation from other sections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-835">每个区域可以作为一个单独的 ASP.NET MVC 项目，然后可由主应用程序引用实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-835">Each area can be implemented as a separate ASP.NET MVC project that can then be referenced by the main application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-836">这可帮助构建大型应用程序时管理复杂性，并使多个团队能够在单个应用程序协同工作更轻松。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-836">This helps manage complexity when you build a large application and makes it easier for multiple teams to work together on a single application.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429276"></a>

### <a name="data-annotation-attribute-validation-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-837">数据注释属性验证支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-837">Data-Annotation Attribute Validation Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-838">*DataAnnotations*属性，您可以通过使用元数据特性附加到模型的验证逻辑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-838">*DataAnnotations* attributes let you attach validation logic to a model by using metadata attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-839">*DataAnnotations*属性在 ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 中的 ASP.NET 动态数据中引入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-839">*DataAnnotations* attributes were introduced in ASP.NET Dynamic Data in ASP.NET 3.5 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-840">这些属性已集成到默认模型联编程序，并且提供元数据驱动的方法来验证用户输入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-840">These attributes have been integrated into the default model binder and provide a metadata-driven means to validate user input.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429277"></a>

### <a name="templated-helpers"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-841">模板化帮助器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-841">Templated Helpers</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-842">模板化帮助器可自动关联的编辑和显示数据类型的模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-842">Templated helpers let you automatically associate edit and display templates with data types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-843">例如，使用模板帮助器来指定自动为呈现日期选取器 UI 元素*System.DateTime*值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-843">For example, you can use a template helper to specify that a date-picker UI element is automatically rendered for a *System.DateTime* value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-844">这是类似于 ASP.NET 动态数据中的字段模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-844">This is similar to field templates in ASP.NET Dynamic Data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-845">*Html.EditorFor*并*Html.DisplayFor*帮助器方法具有的内置支持的呈现标准数据类型具有多个属性也为复杂对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-845">The *Html.EditorFor* and *Html.DisplayFor* helper methods have built-in support for rendering standard data types as well as complex objects with multiple properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-846">它们还通过自定义呈现让您可以之类的数据注释属性*DisplayName*并*ScaffoldColumn*到*ViewModel*对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-846">They also customize rendering by letting you apply data-annotation attributes like *DisplayName* and *ScaffoldColumn* to the *ViewModel* object.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-847">通常，你想要自定义 UI 帮助程序更进一步的输出，并可以完全控制生成的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-847">Often you want to customize the output from UI helpers even further and have complete control over what is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-848">*Html.EditorFor*并*Html.DisplayFor*帮助器方法支持此功能使用模板化机制，允许您定义外部模板，可以重写和控件呈现的输出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-848">The *Html.EditorFor* and *Html.DisplayFor* helper methods support this using a templating mechanism that lets you define external templates that can override and control the output rendered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-849">为类，可以单独呈现模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-849">The templates can be rendered individually for a class.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429278"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304649"></a>

## <a name="dynamic-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-850">Dynamic Data — 动态数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-850">Dynamic Data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-851">引入了动态数据中 2008 年年中的.NET Framework 3.5 SP1 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-851">Dynamic Data was introduced in the .NET Framework 3.5 SP1 release in mid-2008.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-852">此功能提供了用于创建数据驱动的应用程序，其中包括许多增强功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-852">This feature provides many enhancements for creating data-driven applications, including the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-853">用于快速构建数据驱动网站的 RAD 体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-853">A RAD experience for quickly building a data-driven Web site.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-854">基于数据模型中定义的约束的自动验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-854">Automatic validation that is based on constraints defined in the data model.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-855">能够轻松地更改为中的字段生成的标记*GridView*并*DetailsView*使用动态数据项目的一部分的字段模板的控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-855">The ability to easily change the markup that is generated for fields in the *GridView* and *DetailsView* controls by using field templates that are part of your Dynamic Data project.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-856">请注意有关详细信息，请参阅[动态数据文档](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx)MSDN 库中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-856">Note For more information, see the [Dynamic Data documentation](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) in the MSDN Library.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-857">为 ASP.NET 4 中，动态数据得到增强，使开发人员能够更强大的功能来快速构建数据驱动的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-857">For ASP.NET 4, Dynamic Data has been enhanced to give developers even more power for quickly building data-driven Web sites.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429279"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304650"></a>

### <a name="enabling-dynamic-data-for-existing-projects"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-858">对于现有项目中启用动态数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-858">Enabling Dynamic Data for Existing Projects</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-859">在.NET Framework 3.5 SP1 中提供的动态数据功能引入新功能，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-859">Dynamic Data features that shipped in the .NET Framework 3.5 SP1 brought new features such as the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-860">字段模板 – 这些将基于数据类型的模板提供的数据绑定控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-860">Field templates – These provide data-type-based templates for data-bound controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-861">字段模板提供更简单的方法来自定义比使用为每个字段的模板字段的数据控件的外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-861">Field templates provide a simpler way to customize the look of data controls than using template fields for each field.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-862">验证-动态数据，您可以在数据类使用属性来指定为必填的字段范围检查、 类型检查、 使用正则表达式匹配的模式的常见方案的验证和自定义验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-862">Validation – Dynamic Data lets you use attributes on data classes to specify validation for common scenarios like required fields, range checking, type checking, pattern matching using regular expressions, and custom validation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-863">由数据控件强制进行验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-863">Validation is enforced by the data controls.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-864">但是，这些功能具有以下要求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-864">However, these features had the following requirements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-865">数据访问层必须基于 Entity Framework 或 LINQ to SQL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-865">The data-access layer had to be based on Entity Framework or LINQ to SQL.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-866">唯一的数据源控件支持这些功能已*EntityDataSource*或*LinqDataSource*控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-866">The only data source controls supported for these features were the *EntityDataSource* or *LinqDataSource* controls.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-867">功能需要使用动态数据或动态数据实体模板，以支持该功能所需的所有文件已创建的 Web 项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-867">The features required a Web project that had been created using the Dynamic Data or Dynamic Data Entities templates in order to have all the files that were required to support the feature.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-868">在 ASP.NET 4 中的动态数据支持的主要目标是能够为任何 ASP.NET 应用程序的新功能的动态数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-868">A major goal of Dynamic Data support in ASP.NET 4 is to enable the new functionality of Dynamic Data for any ASP.NET application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-869">下面的示例显示了可以在现有页面中充分利用动态数据功能的控件标记的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-869">The following example shows markup for controls that can take advantage of Dynamic Data functionality in an existing page.</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample91.aspx)]

### <a name="support-for-inheritance-in-the-data-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-910">对数据模型中继承的支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-910">Support for Inheritance in the Data Model</span></span>

### <a name="support-for-many-to-many-relationships-entity-framework-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-915">支持多对多关系 （仅适用于实体框架）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-915">Support for Many-to-Many Relationships (Entity Framework Only)</span></span>

### <a name="new-attributes-to-control-display-and-support-enumerations"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-918">新属性来控制显示和支持枚举</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-918">New Attributes to Control Display and Support Enumerations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-919">*DisplayAttribute*已添加为您提供字段的显示方式的更多控制权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-919">The *DisplayAttribute* has been added to give you additional control over how fields are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-920">*DisplayName*早期版本允许你更改用作字段标题的名称的动态数据中的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-920">The *DisplayName* attribute in earlier versions of Dynamic Data allowed you to change the name that is used as a caption for a field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-921">新*DisplayAttribute*类，可以指定用于显示的字段，例如在其中会显示一个字段，以及是否将使用一个字段作为筛选器顺序的更多选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-921">The new *DisplayAttribute* class lets you specify more options for displaying a field, such as the order in which a field is displayed and whether a field will be used as a filter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-922">该属性还提供了用于标签的名称的独立控制*GridView*控制中使用的名称*DetailsView*控件，该字段的帮助文本，水印用于字段 （如果该字段接受输入的文本）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-922">The attribute also provides independent control of the name used for the labels in a *GridView* control, the name used in a *DetailsView* control, the help text for the field, and the watermark used for the field (if the field accepts text input).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-923">*EnumDataTypeAttribute*类已添加，以便你可以将字段映射到枚举。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-923">The *EnumDataTypeAttribute* class has been added to let you map fields to enumerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-924">当此特性应用于字段时，指定枚举类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-924">When you apply this attribute to a field, you specify an enumeration type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-925">动态数据使用新`Enumeration.ascx`的字段模板来创建 UI，以显示和编辑枚举值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-925">Dynamic Data uses the new `Enumeration.ascx` field template to create UI for displaying and editing enumeration values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-926">该模板将映射到枚举中的名称来自数据库的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-926">The template maps the values from the database to the names in the enumeration.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729050"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429287"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304658"></a>

### <a name="enhanced-support-for-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-927">对筛选器的增强的支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-927">Enhanced Support for Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-928">动态数据 1.0 附带了内置布尔值列和外键列的筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-928">Dynamic Data 1.0 shipped with built-in filters for Boolean columns and foreign-key columns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-929">筛选器不允许，可以指定是否显示它们，或以何种顺序显示它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-929">The filters did not allow you to specify whether they were displayed or in what order they were displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-930">新*DisplayAttribute*属性解决了这两的这些问题，请为您提供对某列是否显示为筛选器控制并以什么顺序显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-930">The new *DisplayAttribute* attribute addresses both of these issues by giving you control over whether a column is displayed as a filter and in what order it will be displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-931">其他增强功能是，筛选支持已被重新[编写为使用新](#0.2__QueryExtender "_QueryExtender") Web 窗体的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-931">An additional enhancement is that filtering support has been re[written to use the new](#0.2__QueryExtender "_QueryExtender") feature of Web Forms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-932">这样可以创建筛选器，而无需了解的数据源控件的筛选器将与一起使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-932">This lets you create filters without requiring knowledge of the data source control that the filters will be used with.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-933">这些扩展，以及筛选器也已转换为模板控件，该编辑器可以添加新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-933">Along with these extensions, filters have also been turned into template controls, which allows you to add new ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-934">最后， *DisplayAttribute*前面所述的类允许在相同中重写的默认筛选器的方式*UIHint*允许重写的列的默认字段模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-934">Finally, the *DisplayAttribute* class mentioned earlier allows the default filter to be overridden, in the same way that *UIHint* allows the default field template for a column to be overridden.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729051"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429288"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304659"></a>

## <a name="visual-studio-2010-web-development-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-935">Visual Studio 2010 Web 开发改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-935">Visual Studio 2010 Web Development Improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-936">对于更高版本 CSS 兼容性，通过 HTML 和 ASP.NET 标记代码段和新动态 IntelliSense JavaScript 提高工作效率增强了 Visual Studio 2010 中的 web 开发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-936">Web development in Visual Studio 2010 has been enhanced for greater CSS compatibility, increased productivity through HTML and ASP.NET markup snippets and new dynamic IntelliSense JavaScript.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729052"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429289"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304660"></a>

### <a name="improved-css-compatibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-937">改进的 CSS 兼容性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-937">Improved CSS Compatibility</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-938">Visual Studio 2010 中的 Visual Web Developer 设计器已更新，以提高 CSS 2.1 标准符合性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-938">The Visual Web Developer designer in Visual Studio 2010 has been updated to improve CSS 2.1 standards compliance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-939">在设计器更好地保留在 HTML 源的完整性和 Visual Studio 的早期版本相比更加可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-939">The designer better preserves integrity of the HTML source and is more robust than in previous versions of Visual Studio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-940">实质上，体系结构改进还进行了将会更好地启用中呈现、 布局和可维护性的未来增强功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-940">Under the hood, architectural improvements have also been made that will better enable future enhancements in rendering, layout, and serviceability.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729053"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429290"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304661"></a>

### <a name="html-and-javascript-snippets"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-941">HTML 和 JavaScript 代码片段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-941">HTML and JavaScript Snippets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-942">在 HTML 编辑器中，IntelliSense 会自动完成的标记名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-942">In the HTML editor, IntelliSense auto-completes tag names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-943">IntelliSense 代码段功能会自动完成整个标记和的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-943">The IntelliSense Snippets feature auto-completes entire tags and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-944">在 Visual Studio 2010 中，IntelliSense 代码段支持 JavaScript 以及 C# 和 Visual Basic 中，这在 Visual Studio 的早期版本中受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-944">In Visual Studio 2010, IntelliSense snippets are supported for JavaScript, alongside C# and Visual Basic, which were supported in earlier versions of Visual Studio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-945">Visual Studio 2010 包括了超过 200 个代码段，可帮助你自动完成常见 ASP.NET 和 HTML 标记，包括必需的属性 (如 runat ="server") 和特定于标记的公共属性 (如*ID*， *DataSourceID*， *ControlToValidate*，和*文本*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-945">Visual Studio 2010 includes over 200 snippets that help you auto-complete common ASP.NET and HTML tags, including required attributes (such as runat="server") and common attributes specific to a tag (such as *ID*, *DataSourceID*, *ControlToValidate*, and *Text*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-946">您可以下载其他代码段，也可以编写您自己封装的你或你的团队使用的常见任务的标记块的代码段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-946">You can download additional snippets, or you can write your own snippets that encapsulate the blocks of markup that you or your team use for common tasks.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729054"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429291"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304662"></a>

### <a name="javascript-intellisense-enhancements"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-947">JavaScript IntelliSense 增强功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-947">JavaScript IntelliSense Enhancements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-948">在 Visual 2010 中，JavaScript IntelliSense 经过重新设计，提供更丰富的编辑体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-948">In Visual 2010, JavaScript IntelliSense has been redesigned to provide an even richer editing experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-949">IntelliSense 现在可识别具有已动态生成的方法如对象*registerNamespace*和类似的技术使用的其他 JavaScript 框架。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-949">IntelliSense now recognizes objects that have been dynamically generated by methods such as *registerNamespace* and by similar techniques used by other JavaScript frameworks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-950">要分析的脚本的大型库并使用很少或没有处理延迟显示 IntelliSense 改进了性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-950">Performance has been improved to analyze large libraries of script and to display IntelliSense with little or no processing delay.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-951">若要支持几乎所有第三方库，并以支持各种编码风格已极大地增加兼容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-951">Compatibility has been dramatically increased to support nearly all third-party libraries and to support diverse coding styles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-952">键入并立即利用 intellisense 时，现在进行分析文档注释。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-952">Documentation comments are now parsed as you type and are immediately leveraged by IntelliSense.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729055"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429292"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304663"></a>

## <a name="web-application-deployment-with-visual-studio-2010"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-953">使用 Visual Studio 2010 的 web 应用程序部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-953">Web Application Deployment with Visual Studio 2010</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-954">当 ASP.NET 开发人员部署 Web 应用程序时，他们经常发现他们会遇到以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-954">When ASP.NET developers deploy a Web application, they often find that they encounter issues such as the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-955">部署到共享的托管站点需要技术，例如 FTP，可能会很慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-955">Deploying to a shared hosting site requires technologies such as FTP, which can be slow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-956">此外，你必须手动执行任务，例如运行 SQL 脚本来配置数据库，必须更改 IIS 设置，例如，为应用程序中配置虚拟目录文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-956">In addition, you must manually perform tasks such as running SQL scripts to configure a database and you must change IIS settings, such as configuring a virtual directory folder as an application.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-957">在企业环境中，除了部署 Web 应用程序文件，管理员经常必须修改 ASP.NET 配置文件和 IIS 设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-957">In an enterprise environment, in addition to deploying the Web application files, administrators frequently must modify ASP.NET configuration files and IIS settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-958">数据库管理员必须运行一系列 SQL 脚本来获取运行的应用程序数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-958">Database administrators must run a series of SQL scripts to get the application database running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-959">此类安装耗费大量精力，通常需要数小时才能完成，并且必须仔细记载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-959">Such installations are labor intensive, often take hours to complete, and must be carefully documented.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-960">Visual Studio 2010 包括解决这些问题，以及允许用户无缝地将部署 Web 应用程序的技术。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-960">Visual Studio 2010 includes technologies that address these issues and that let you seamlessly deploy Web applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-961">这些技术之一是 IIS Web 部署工具 (MsDeploy.exe)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-961">One of these technologies is the IIS Web Deployment Tool (MsDeploy.exe).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-962">Visual Studio 2010 中的 web 部署功能包括以下主要方面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-962">Web deployment features in Visual Studio 2010 include the following major areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-963">Web 打包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-963">Web packaging</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-964">Web.config 转换</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-964">Web.config transformation</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-965">数据库部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-965">Database deployment</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-966">单击发布为 Web 应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-966">One-click publish for Web applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-967">以下部分提供有关这些功能的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-967">The following sections provide details about these features.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729056"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429293"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304664"></a>

### <a name="web-packaging"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-968">Web 打包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-968">Web Packaging</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-969">Visual Studio 2010 使用 MSDeploy 工具来创建应用程序，这被称为一个压缩 (.zip) 文件*Web 包*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-969">Visual Studio 2010 uses the MSDeploy tool to create a compressed (.zip) file for your application, which is referred to as a *Web package*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-970">包文件包含有关你的应用程序以及以下内容的元数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-970">The package file contains metadata about your application plus the following content:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-971">IIS 设置，其中包括应用程序池设置、 错误页设置等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-971">IIS settings, which includes application pool settings, error page settings, and so on.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-972">实际 Web 内容，其中包括 Web 页面、 用户控件、 静态内容 （映像和 HTML 文件） 等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-972">The actual Web content, which includes Web pages, user controls, static content (images and HTML files), and so on.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-973">SQL Server 数据库架构和数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-973">SQL Server database schemas and data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-974">安全证书，组件安装在 GAC、 注册表设置等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-974">Security certificates, components to install in the GAC, registry settings, and so on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-975">可以复制到任何服务器，然后通过使用 IIS 管理器手动安装 Web 包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-975">A Web package can be copied to any server and then installed manually by using IIS Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-976">或者，对于自动部署，包可安装使用命令行命令或使用部署 Api。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-976">Alternatively, for automated deployment, the package can be installed by using command-line commands or by using deployment APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-977">Visual Studio 2010 提供了内置的 MSBuild 任务和目标以创建 Web 包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-977">Visual Studio 2010 provides built in MSBuild tasks and targets to create Web packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-978">有关详细信息，请参阅[ASP.NET Web 应用程序项目部署概述](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd394698%28VS.100%29.aspx)MSDN 网站上和[10 + 20 原因为何应创建 Web 包](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/07/10-20-reasons-why-you-should-create-web.html)在 Vishal Joshi 博客上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-978">For more information, see [ASP.NET Web Application Project Deployment Overview](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd394698%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [10 + 20 reasons why you should create a Web Package](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/07/10-20-reasons-why-you-should-create-web.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729057"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429294"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304665"></a>

### <a name="webconfig-transformation"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-979">Web.config 转换</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-979">Web.config Transformation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-980">对于 Web 应用程序部署，Visual Studio 2010 引入了[XML 文档转换 (XDT)](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)，这是一项功能，允许你转换`Web.config`开发设置中为生产设置的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-980">For Web application deployment, Visual Studio 2010 introduces [XML Document Transform (XDT)](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html), which is a feature that lets you transform a `Web.config` file from development settings to production settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-981">转换设置名为的转换文件中指定`web.debug.config`， `web.release.config`，依次类推。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-981">Transformation settings are specified in transform files named `web.debug.config`, `web.release.config`, and so on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-982">（这些文件的名称匹配 MSBuild 配置。）转换文件包括只是需要对已部署进行的更改`Web.config`文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-982">(The names of these files match MSBuild configurations.) A transform file includes just the changes that you need to make to a deployed `Web.config` file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-983">使用简单的语法指定所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-983">You specify the changes by using simple syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-984">下面的示例显示了一部分`web.release.config`可能生成部署的发布配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-984">The following example shows a portion of a `web.release.config` file that might be produced for deployment of your release configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-985">在示例中的替换关键字在部署过程中指定*connectionString*中的节点`Web.config`文件将替换示例中列出的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-985">The Replace keyword in the example specifies that during deployment the *connectionString* node in the `Web.config` file will be replaced with the values that are listed in the example.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-986">有关详细信息，请参阅[Web 应用程序项目部署的 Web.config 转换语法](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465326%28VS.100%29.aspx)msdn <a id="0.2_a"> </a> Web 站点和[Web 部署：Web.Config 转换](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)在 Vishal Joshi 博客上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-986">For more information, see [Web.config Transformation Syntax for Web Application Project Deployment](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465326%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN <a id="0.2_a"></a> Web site and[Web Deployment: Web.Config Transformation](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

### <a name="database-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-987">数据库部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-987">Database Deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-988">Visual Studio 2010 部署包可以包含 SQL Server 数据库上的依赖项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-988">A Visual Studio 2010 deployment package can include dependencies on SQL Server databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-989">为包定义的一部分，为源数据库提供连接字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-989">As part of the package definition, you provide the connection string for your source database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-990">创建 Web 包时，Visual Studio 2010 创建 SQL 脚本 （可选） 为数据库架构和数据，，然后添加到包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-990">When you create the Web package, Visual Studio 2010 creates SQL scripts for the database schema and optionally for the data, and then adds these to the package.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-991">此外可以提供自定义 SQL 脚本，并指定其应运行在服务器的序列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-991">You can also provide custom SQL scripts and specify the sequence in which they should run on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-992">在部署时，提供了适合于目标服务器; 一个连接字符串然后，部署过程使用此连接字符串来运行脚本，创建数据库架构，并添加数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-992">At deployment time, you provide a connection string that is appropriate for the target server; the deployment process then uses this connection string to run the scripts that create the database schema and add the data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-993">此外，通过使用一次单击发布，您可以配置部署应用程序发布到远程共享托管站点时，直接发布你的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-993">In addition, by using one-click publish, you can configure deployment to publish your database directly when the application is published to a remote shared hosting site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-994">有关详细信息，请参阅[如何：部署数据库与 Web 应用程序项目](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465343%28VS.100%29.aspx)MSDN 网站上和[VS 2010 使用的数据库部署](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)在 Vishal Joshi 博客上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-994">For more information, see [How to: Deploy a Database With a Web Application Project](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465343%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [Database Deployment with VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729059"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429296"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304667"></a>

### <a name="one-click-publish-for-web-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-995">单击发布为 Web 应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-995">One-Click Publish for Web Applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-996">Visual Studio 2010 还允许您使用的 IIS 远程管理服务发布到远程服务器的 Web 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-996">Visual Studio 2010 also lets you use the IIS remote management service to publish a Web application to a remote server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-997">为你的托管帐户或测试服务器或暂存服务器，可以创建发布配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-997">You can create a publish profile for your hosting account or for testing servers or staging servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-998">每个配置文件可以安全地保存相应的凭据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-998">Each profile can save appropriate credentials securely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-999">你可以随后部署到任何目标服务器通过使用 Web 一次单击一次单击发布工具栏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-999">You can then deploy to any of the target servers with one click by using the Web one-click publish toolbar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1000">使用 Visual Studio 2010，您还可以通过使用 MSBuild 命令行发布。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1000">With Visual Studio 2010, you can also publish by using the MSBuild command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1001">这允许您配置您的团队生成环境，以持续集成模型中包括发布。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1001">This lets you configure your team build environment to include publishing in a continuous-integration model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1002">有关详细信息，请参阅[如何：部署 Web 应用程序项目使用一键式发布和 Web 部署](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465337%28VS.100%29.aspx)MSDN 网站上和[Web 一键式发布使用 VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/05/web-1-click-publish-with-vs-2010.html)在 Vishal Joshi 博客上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1002">For more information, see [How to: Deploy a Web Application Project Using One-Click Publish and Web Deploy](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465337%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [Web 1-Click Publish with VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/05/web-1-click-publish-with-vs-2010.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1003">若要在 Visual Studio 2010 中查看有关 Web 应用程序部署的视频演示，请参阅[VS 2010 Web 开发人员预览版](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2008/12/vs-2010-for-web-developer-previews.html)在 Vishal Joshi 博客上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1003">To view video presentations about Web application deployment in Visual Studio 2010, see [VS 2010 for Web Developer Previews](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2008/12/vs-2010-for-web-developer-previews.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

### <a name="resources"></a><span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1004">资源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1004">Resources</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1005">以下网站提供有关 ASP.NET 4 和 Visual Studio 2010 的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1005">The following Web sites provide additional information about ASP.NET 4 and Visual Studio 2010.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1006">[ASP.NET 4](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/ee532866%28VS.100%29.aspx) — MSDN 网站上的 ASP.NET 4 的官方文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1006">[ASP.NET 4](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/ee532866%28VS.100%29.aspx) — The official documentation for ASP.NET 4 on the MSDN Web site.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1007">[https://www.asp.net/](https://www.asp.net/) — ASP.NET 团队的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1007">[https://www.asp.net/](https://www.asp.net/) — The ASP.NET team's own Web site.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1008">[https://www.asp.net/dynamicdata/](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) 并[ASP.NET 动态数据内容映射](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545%28VS.100%29.aspx)— ASP.NET 团队网站和 ASP.NET 动态数据有关的正式文档中的在线资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1008">[https://www.asp.net/dynamicdata/](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) and [ASP.NET Dynamic Data Content Map](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545%28VS.100%29.aspx) — Online resources on the ASP.NET team site and in the official documentation for ASP.NET Dynamic Data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1009">[https://www.asp.net/ajax/](../../ajax/index.md) — ASP.NET Ajax 开发主 Web 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1009">[https://www.asp.net/ajax/](../../ajax/index.md) — The main Web resource for ASP.NET Ajax development.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1010">[https://blogs.msdn.com/webdevtools/](https://blogs.msdn.com/webdevtools/) — Visual Studio 2010 中包括有关功能的信息 Visual Web 开发人员团队博客。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1010">[https://blogs.msdn.com/webdevtools/](https://blogs.msdn.com/webdevtools/) — The Visual Web Developer Team blog, which includes information about features in Visual Studio 2010.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="e93fb-1011">[ASP.NET WebStack](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetWebStack) — ASP.NET 的预览版本的主要 Web 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e93fb-1011">[ASP.NET WebStack](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetWebStack) — The main Web resource for preview releases of ASP.NET.</span></span>
